<td>\n         Scrubbed\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         ---\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Weather\n        </td>\n        <td>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         30%\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cbs1209_21-0">\n          <a href="#cite_note-cbs1209-21">\n           [21]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         NASA opted for 48-hour turnaround instead of 24 due to 10% go weather forecast for 8 December 2006\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cbs1209_21-1">\n          <a href="#cite_note-cbs1209-21">\n           [21]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         2\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none;">\n          2006-12-09 20:47:35 !\n         </span>\n         <span class="sorttext">\n          9 Dec 2006, 8:47:35 pm\n         </span>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Success\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         1 day, 23 hours, 12 minutes\n        </td>\n        <td>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         70%\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22">\n          <a href="#cite_note-22">\n           [22]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="9_December_(Flight_day_1_\xe2\x80\x93_Launch)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="9_December_.28Flight_day_1_.E2.80.93_Launch.29">\n        9 December (Flight day 1 \xe2\x80\x93 Launch)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-116&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 9 December (Flight day 1 \xe2\x80\x93 Launch)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Sts116-launch.png">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3000" data-file-width="2037" height="324" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/35/Sts116-launch.png/220px-Sts116-launch.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/35/Sts116-launch.png/330px-Sts116-launch.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/35/Sts116-launch.png/440px-Sts116-launch.png 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Sts116-launch.png" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <i>\n          Discovery\n         </i>\n         at liftoff\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-116_rocket_boosters_(NASA_KSC-06PD-2794).jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2014" data-file-width="3000" height="148" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/66/STS-116_rocket_boosters_%28NASA_KSC-06PD-2794%29.jpg/220px-STS-116_rocket_boosters_%28NASA_KSC-06PD-2794%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/66/STS-116_rocket_boosters_%28NASA_KSC-06PD-2794%29.jpg/330px-STS-116_rocket_boosters_%28NASA_KSC-06PD-2794%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/66/STS-116_rocket_boosters_%28NASA_KSC-06PD-2794%29.jpg/440px-STS-116_rocket_boosters_%28NASA_KSC-06PD-2794%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-116_rocket_boosters_(NASA_KSC-06PD-2794).jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         The\n         <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Solid_Rocket_Booster" title="Space Shuttle Solid Rocket Booster">\n          solid rocket boosters\n         </a>\n         being retrieved from the Atlantic Ocean after the takeoff of STS-116.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       lifted off successfully at 8:47\xc2\xa0pm\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Eastern_Time_Zone_(North_America)" title="Eastern Time Zone (North America)">\n        EST\n       </a>\n       (01:47\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UTC" title="UTC">\n        UTC\n       </a>\n       ), lighting up the Florida\'s coastline. Weather conditions \xe2\x80\x93 in particular crosswinds at the launch and landing sites \xe2\x80\x93 continued to trend positively in the hours approaching the launch window Saturday night. The fueling process for Discovery\'s external tanks began at 12:46 EST (17:46 UTC) and was completed at approximately 15:45 EST (20:45 UTC). If a\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_abort_modes#Intact_abort_modes" title="Space Shuttle abort modes">\n        transatlantic abort landing\n       </a>\n       (TAL) had been required during ascent, the shuttle had three possible landing sites:\n       <a href="/wiki/Zaragoza_Airport" title="Zaragoza Airport">\n        Zaragoza\n       </a>\n       or\n       <a href="/wiki/Mor%C3%B3n_Air_Base" title="Mor\xc3\xb3n Air Base">\n        Mor\xc3\xb3n Air Base\n       </a>\n       in Spain, or\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Istres_Air_Base" title="Istres Air Base">\n        Istres\n       </a>\n       , France.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23">\n        <a href="#cite_note-23">\n         [23]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The launch was the third shuttle mission in five months, being preceded by\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-121" title="STS-121">\n        STS-121\n       </a>\n       in July and\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-115" title="STS-115">\n        STS-115\n       </a>\n       in September, and was the first night launch in four years since\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-113" title="STS-113">\n        STS-113\n       </a>\n       and first night launch following the Columbia accident during\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-107" title="STS-107">\n        STS-107\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="10_December_(Flight_day_2)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="10_December_.28Flight_day_2.29">\n        10 December (Flight day 2)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-116&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: 10 December (Flight day 2)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Flight day 2 began for the astronauts at 15:47 UTC. The first order of business for the day was a thorough inspection of the Shuttle. Using sensors and cameras attached to a fifty-foot boom, which was in turn connected to a fifty-foot robotic arm, Nicholas Patrick inspected the leading edge of the wings and the nose cap. The process, which took five and a half hours, suffered a minor glitch that required Patrick to order the arm to manually grab the boom. During this time, the crew also inspected the upper surface of the orbiter.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-spacecomdaytwo_24-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-spacecomdaytwo-24">\n         [24]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Astronauts also completed a check of the spacesuits to be used during the mission, along with preparation for docking with the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">\n        International Space Station\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-116_Payload_(NASA_S116-E-05364).jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1876" data-file-width="2836" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/47/STS-116_Payload_%28NASA_S116-E-05364%29.jpg/220px-STS-116_Payload_%28NASA_S116-E-05364%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/47/STS-116_Payload_%28NASA_S116-E-05364%29.jpg/330px-STS-116_Payload_%28NASA_S116-E-05364%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/47/STS-116_Payload_%28NASA_S116-E-05364%29.jpg/440px-STS-116_Payload_%28NASA_S116-E-05364%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-116_Payload_(NASA_S116-E-05364).jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         As seen through windows on the aft flight deck of Space Shuttle Discovery, the\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Payload_(air_and_space_craft)" title="Payload (air and space craft)">\n          payload\n         </a>\n         bay is featured in this image photographed by a STS-116 Crewmember.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="11_December_(Flight_day_3_\xe2\x80\x93_Docking_to_ISS)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="11_December_.28Flight_day_3_.E2.80.93_Docking_to_ISS.29">\n        11 December (Flight day 3 \xe2\x80\x93 Docking to ISS)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-116&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: 11 December (Flight day 3 \xe2\x80\x93 Docking to ISS)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Flight day 3 began for the astronauts at 15:18\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UTC" title="UTC">\n        UTC\n       </a>\n       . Following the\n       <a href="/wiki/Rendezvous_pitch_maneuver" title="Rendezvous pitch maneuver">\n        rendezvous pitch maneuver\n       </a>\n       , docking to the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">\n        International Space Station\n       </a>\n       occurred at 22:12 UTC. The hatch between the International Space Station and\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       was opened at 23:54 UTC.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25">\n        <a href="#cite_note-25">\n         [25]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The joint ISS/Shuttle crew then worked to undertake some further detailed inspection of the orbiter and unloaded the P5 truss segment from the payload bay, handing it off successfully from the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Remote_Manipulator_System" title="Remote Manipulator System">\n        shuttle robotic arm\n       </a>\n       to the\n       <a href="/wiki/Mobile_Servicing_System" title="Mobile Servicing System">\n        station arm\n       </a>\n       . The astronauts scheduled for Day 4\'s\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Extra-vehicular_activity" title="Extra-vehicular activity">\n        EVA\n       </a>\n       , Robert Curbeam and Christer Fuglesang, ended their day by entering the airlock for a "campout" sleep session to prepare for the EVA by purging their bodies of nitrogen in a lower-pressure environment.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26">\n        <a href="#cite_note-26">\n         [26]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Such a practice is common in order for the astronauts to avoid getting\n       <a href="/wiki/Decompression_sickness" title="Decompression sickness">\n        decompression sickness\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="12_December_(Flight_day_4_\xe2\x80\x93_EVA_#1)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="12_December_.28Flight_day_4_.E2.80.93_EVA_.231.29">\n        12 December (Flight day 4 \xe2\x80\x93 EVA #1)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-116&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: 12 December (Flight day 4 \xe2\x80\x93 EVA #1)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-116_-_P5_Truss_hand-off_to_ISS_(NASA_S116-E-05765).jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2000" data-file-width="3032" height="145" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/STS-116_-_P5_Truss_hand-off_to_ISS_%28NASA_S116-E-05765%29.jpg/220px-STS-116_-_P5_Truss_hand-off_to_ISS_%28NASA_S116-E-05765%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/STS-116_-_P5_Truss_hand-off_to_ISS_%28NASA_S116-E-05765%29.jpg/330px-STS-116_-_P5_Truss_hand-off_to_ISS_%28NASA_S116-E-05765%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/STS-116_-_P5_Truss_hand-off_to_ISS_%28NASA_S116-E-05765%29.jpg/440px-STS-116_-_P5_Truss_hand-off_to_ISS_%28NASA_S116-E-05765%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-116_-_P5_Truss_hand-off_to_ISS_(NASA_S116-E-05765).jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Discovery" title="Space Shuttle Discovery">\n          Space Shuttle\n          <i>\n           Discovery\n          </i>\n         </a>\n         \'s\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Remote_Manipulator_System" title="Remote Manipulator System">\n          Canadarm-1\n         </a>\n         robotic arm hands off the P5 truss section to the International Space Station\'s\n         <a href="/wiki/Mobile_Servicing_System" title="Mobile Servicing System">\n          Canadarm-2\n         </a>\n         during shuttle mission STS-116 in December 2006.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-116_spacewalk_1.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2000" data-file-width="3032" height="145" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/STS-116_spacewalk_1.jpg/220px-STS-116_spacewalk_1.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/STS-116_spacewalk_1.jpg/330px-STS-116_spacewalk_1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/STS-116_spacewalk_1.jpg/440px-STS-116_spacewalk_1.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-116_spacewalk_1.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         While flying over New Zealand, Robert L. Curbeam, Jr. and Christer Fuglesang participate in the mission\'s first spacewalk.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Flight day 4 began for the astronauts at 15:47 UTC.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fday3preview_27-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fday3preview-27">\n         [27]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       During the first\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Extra-vehicular_activity" title="Extra-vehicular activity">\n        EVA\n       </a>\n       of the mission, the astronauts of STS-116 brought the ISS one step closer to completion with the addition of the P5 truss segment.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The EVA began at 20:31 UTC, with Curbeam and Fuglesang removing launch restraints from the P5 truss and Mission Specialist Joan Higginbotham making use of the station\'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Mobile_Servicing_System" title="Mobile Servicing System">\n        robotic arm\n       </a>\n       (the\n       <i>\n        Canadarm2\n       </i>\n       ) to move the truss segment to within inches of its new position on the P4 truss. The spacewalkers then guided Higginbotham with visual cues as the precise operation to finalize the attachment of the truss was completed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28">\n        <a href="#cite_note-28">\n         [28]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       After the P5\xe2\x80\x99s attachment, Curbeam and Fuglesang finalized the installation with power, data and heater cable connections. They also replaced a faulty video camera attached to the\n       <a href="/wiki/Integrated_Truss_Structure#P1.2C_S1_trusses" title="Integrated Truss Structure">\n        S1 truss\n       </a>\n       . Since they worked ahead of the time-line, the two astronauts were also able to complete some get-ahead tasks.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       At the end of the spacewalk, Curbeam congratulated the\n       <a href="/wiki/Nobel_Prize" title="Nobel Prize">\n        Nobel Prize\n       </a>\n       winners, including scientist Dr.\n       <a href="/wiki/John_C._Mather" title="John C. Mather">\n        John C. Mather\n       </a>\n       at NASA\xe2\x80\x99s\n       <a href="/wiki/Goddard_Space_Flight_Center" title="Goddard Space Flight Center">\n        Goddard Space Flight Center\n       </a>\n       in Greenbelt, Maryland.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-flightdayfour_29-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-flightdayfour-29">\n         [29]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Mather was honored for his work on the big-bang theory. Christer Fuglesang also held a short speech in Swedish, encouraging Swedes and others to aspire to become future astronauts. The EVA concluded at 03:07 UTC on the morning of 13 December, and lasted for 6 hours and 36 minutes in total.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-flightdayfour_29-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-flightdayfour-29">\n         [29]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       During the spacewalk, after taking a close look at imagery gathered on the first three days of the flight, mission managers determined that the shuttle\xe2\x80\x99s heat shield would support a safe return to Earth. They also decided a more detailed inspection that had been scheduled for later in the mission would not be necessary.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Three more spacewalks, one of which was unplanned, were required to reconfigure and redistribute power on the station, so that the solar arrays installed during\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-115" title="STS-115">\n        STS-115\n       </a>\n       could be used. The first step of reconfiguring the power took place Wednesday when the port solar array on the P6 truss will be retracted, which allowed the activation and rotation of the Solar Alpha Rotary Joint on the P4. The rotary joint allows the solar arrays on the P4 to track the sun.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The astronauts were required to spend the night sleeping in protected areas in order to avoid radiation from a solar flare eruption.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30">\n        <a href="#cite_note-30">\n         [30]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="13_December_(Flight_day_5_\xe2\x80\x93_Solar_Array_Reorganization)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="13_December_.28Flight_day_5_.E2.80.93_Solar_Array_Reorganization.29">\n        13 December (Flight day 5 \xe2\x80\x93 Solar Array Reorganization)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-116&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: 13 December (Flight day 5 \xe2\x80\x93 Solar Array Reorganization)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-116_solar_panel_jam.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2000" data-file-width="3032" height="145" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4a/STS-116_solar_panel_jam.jpg/220px-STS-116_solar_panel_jam.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4a/STS-116_solar_panel_jam.jpg/330px-STS-116_solar_panel_jam.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4a/STS-116_solar_panel_jam.jpg/440px-STS-116_solar_panel_jam.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-116_solar_panel_jam.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         A kink that occurred in the port-side P6 solar array during the first attempt to retract that array on 13 December.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Flight day 5 began for the astronauts at 15:21 UTC.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fday5preview_31-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fday5preview-31">\n         [31]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The most high-profile activity was the attempted retraction of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Integrated_Truss_Structure#P6.2C_S6_trusses" title="Integrated Truss Structure">\n        P6\n       </a>\n       port-side\n       <a href="/wiki/Integrated_Truss_Structure#Solar_arrays" title="Integrated Truss Structure">\n        solar array\n       </a>\n       . The process began at 18:28 UTC, but problems with the array folding due to \'kinks\' and \'billows\' led the controllers to redeploy the array (from about 40% retracted). There then followed a series of more than 40 commands to furl and unfurl the arrays in an effort to get them properly aligned and folded.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       At 00:50 UTC, the retraction efforts were abandoned for the day. The problems, which appear to have been caused by a loss of tension in the solar array guide wires,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32">\n        <a href="#cite_note-32">\n         [32]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       had still not been solved, although 14 of the 31 bays on the array had been retracted (leaving 17 bays extended). This was enough to leave the port side arrays in a safe position to commence the activation of the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Solar_Alpha_Rotary_Joint" title="Solar Alpha Rotary Joint">\n        Solar Alpha Rotary Joint\n       </a>\n       (SARJ) at 01:00 UTC, allowing the solar arrays on the\n       <a href="/wiki/Integrated_Truss_Structure#P3.2FP4.2C_S3.2FS4_truss_assemblies" title="Integrated Truss Structure">\n        P3/P4\n       </a>\n       truss to rotate to follow the sun.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33">\n        <a href="#cite_note-33">\n         [33]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="14_December_(Flight_day_6_\xe2\x80\x93_EVA_#2)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="14_December_.28Flight_day_6_.E2.80.93_EVA_.232.29">\n        14 December (Flight day 6 \xe2\x80\x93 EVA #2)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-116&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: 14 December (Flight day 6 \xe2\x80\x93 EVA #2)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-116_spacewalk_2.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2000" data-file-width="3032" height="145" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ac/STS-116_spacewalk_2.jpg/220px-STS-116_spacewalk_2.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ac/STS-116_spacewalk_2.jpg/330px-STS-116_spacewalk_2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ac/STS-116_spacewalk_2.jpg/440px-STS-116_spacewalk_2.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-116_spacewalk_2.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Christer Fuglesang participates in the mission\'s second session of extravehicular activity.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Flight day 6 began for the astronauts at 15:19 UTC. The day\'s primary activity,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Extra-vehicular_activity" title="Extra-vehicular activity">\n        EVA\n       </a>\n       No. 2, began rewiring work to bring the station\'s permanent electrical power systems into use. To allow this changeover, station controllers had to power down about half the systems on the ISS. The EVA started at 19:41 UTC with Bob Curbeam and Christer Fuglesang exiting the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Joint_Airlock" title="Joint Airlock">\n        Quest airlock\n       </a>\n       , 30 minutes early. EVA No. 2 was planned to activate channels 2 and 3 of the four-channel electrical system, and the work progressed smoothly. About two hours into the spacewalk the first current was flowing through the reconfigured system, using the power from the P4 solar arrays for the first time. The EVA was completed in exactly 5 hours, finishing at 00:41 UTC.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FD6report_34-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-FD6report-34">\n         [34]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="15_December_(Flight_day_7)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="15_December_.28Flight_day_7.29">\n        15 December (Flight day 7)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-116&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: 15 December (Flight day 7)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-116_%2B_Expedition14_CrewMembers_(NASA_S116-E-06472).jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2000" data-file-width="3032" height="145" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/STS-116_%2B_Expedition14_CrewMembers_%28NASA_S116-E-06472%29.jpg/220px-STS-116_%2B_Expedition14_CrewMembers_%28NASA_S116-E-06472%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/STS-116_%2B_Expedition14_CrewMembers_%28NASA_S116-E-06472%29.jpg/330px-STS-116_%2B_Expedition14_CrewMembers_%28NASA_S116-E-06472%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/85/STS-116_%2B_Expedition14_CrewMembers_%28NASA_S116-E-06472%29.jpg/440px-STS-116_%2B_Expedition14_CrewMembers_%28NASA_S116-E-06472%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-116_%2B_Expedition14_CrewMembers_(NASA_S116-E-06472).jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Crew photo.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Flight day 7 was a light work day for the crews of\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Discovery" title="Space Shuttle Discovery">\n        Discovery\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">\n        ISS\n       </a>\n       after the previous days\' activities. Spacewalkers Bob Curbeam and Christer Fuglesang enjoyed some\n       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_U.S._Army_acronyms_and_expressions&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="List of U.S. Army acronyms and expressions (page does not exist)">\n        R&amp;R\n       </a>\n       , while the rest of the crew performed cleanup and preparatory tasks for Flight day 8\'s planned\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Extra-vehicular_activity" title="Extra-vehicular activity">\n        EVA\n       </a>\n       #3. The traditional joint photo session and joint news conference were held by the crews.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-116flightplan_35-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-116flightplan-35">\n         [35]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       During this event Swedish first time astronaut Christer Fuglesang was interviewed by\n       <a href="/wiki/Victoria,_Crown_Princess_of_Sweden" title="Victoria, Crown Princess of Sweden">\n        Crown Princess Victoria\n       </a>\n       and also set a 20-second Frisbee world record in space, broadcast live on Swedish\n       <a href="/wiki/TV4_(Sweden)" title="TV4 (Sweden)">\n        TV4\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-36">\n        <a href="#cite_note-36">\n         [36]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37">\n        <a href="#cite_note-37">\n         [37]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In an attempt to free a stuck solar panel, Thomas Reiter exercised vigorously on a machine which is known to cause oscillations in the solar arrays; it was not successful. Mission controllers continued to look at other solutions to the solar panel folding problem so as to enable complete retraction, including an extended or additional EVA.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-38">\n        <a href="#cite_note-38">\n         [38]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="16_December_(Flight_day_8_\xe2\x80\x93_EVA_#3)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="16_December_.28Flight_day_8_.E2.80.93_EVA_.233.29">\n        16 December (Flight day 8 \xe2\x80\x93 EVA #3)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-116&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: 16 December (Flight day 8 \xe2\x80\x93 EVA #3)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-116_Solar_Panel_Spacewalk.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2008" data-file-width="3032" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/33/STS-116_Solar_Panel_Spacewalk.jpg/220px-STS-116_Solar_Panel_Spacewalk.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/33/STS-116_Solar_Panel_Spacewalk.jpg/330px-STS-116_Solar_Panel_Spacewalk.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/33/STS-116_Solar_Panel_Spacewalk.jpg/440px-STS-116_Solar_Panel_Spacewalk.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-116_Solar_Panel_Spacewalk.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Astronaut Robert L. Curbeam Jr., STS-116 mission specialist, works with the port overhead solar array wing on the International Space Station\'s P6 truss during the mission\'s fourth session of extravehicular activity.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Flight day 8 began for the astronauts at 14:48 UTC. Astronauts Bob Curbeam and \'Suni\' Williams completed the rewiring work on the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">\n        International Space Station\n       </a>\n       . The EVA began at 19:25 UTC and proceeded normally. As an "add-on task" to the EVA, astronauts Curbeam and Williams also continued work on the retraction of a sticking solar array, enabling the retraction of another six sections of the P6 array. At the end of the EVA there were another 11 "bays", or 35% left to retract. Upon completion of the EVA, the astronauts returned to the ISS via the Quest airlock.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-STS116_mission_status_39-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-STS116_mission_status-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Another significant event during the EVA was the\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_debris" title="Space debris">\n        loss of \'Suni\' Williams\' digital camera\n       </a>\n       . At the post-EVA press conference it was suggested that a tether got snagged and caused the camera release button to break off allowing the camera to fall out of its holder. Images were lost but it was determined there was no need to retake them. Curbeam later said to the MCC: "We\'ve got the bracket and the tether. Looks like the screws [on the bracket] came loose, we have the screws and the bracket and the tether."\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ReferenceA_40-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ReferenceA-40">\n         [40]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="17_December_(Flight_day_9)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="17_December_.28Flight_day_9.29">\n        17 December (Flight day 9)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-116&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: 17 December (Flight day 9)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-116_flight_deck.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2000" data-file-width="3032" height="145" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/STS-116_flight_deck.jpg/220px-STS-116_flight_deck.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/STS-116_flight_deck.jpg/330px-STS-116_flight_deck.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/STS-116_flight_deck.jpg/440px-STS-116_flight_deck.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-116_flight_deck.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Flight deck of\n         <i>\n          Discovery\n         </i>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Flight day 9 was mainly spent preparing for EVA #4. The space suits were prepared (adjusting sizes and replacing LiOH canisters) and the crew went through the new procedures which had been developed for attempting to enable the solar array retraction. Various tools were to be coated in kapton tape to protect the array from coming into direct contact with sharp metallic objects and to provide electrical insulation if they are used to manipulate the arrays during the EVA.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ReferenceA_40-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ReferenceA-40">\n         [40]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41">\n        <a href="#cite_note-41">\n         [41]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="18_December_(Flight_day_10_\xe2\x80\x93_EVA_#4)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="18_December_.28Flight_day_10_.E2.80.93_EVA_.234.29">\n        18 December (Flight day 10 \xe2\x80\x93 EVA #4)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-116&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: 18 December (Flight day 10 \xe2\x80\x93 EVA #4)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Flight day 10 began for the astronauts at 14:17 UTC.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-STS116_mission_status_39-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-STS116_mission_status-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Bob Curbeam and Christer Fuglesang embarked on an added\n       <a href="/wiki/Extravehicular_activity" title="Extravehicular activity">\n        EVA\n       </a>\n       at 17:12 UTC to try to fully close the last eleven bays of the balky P6-port Solar Array Wing.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42">\n        <a href="#cite_note-42">\n         [42]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The rapidly planned EVA was successfully completed after a 6-hour 38-minute spacewalk.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NASA_FD10_status_43-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NASA_FD10_status-43">\n         [43]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       At the end of EVA No. 4, Curbeam ranked fifth in total EVA time for U.S. astronauts and 14th overall.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EVA_List_44-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-EVA_List-44">\n         [44]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="19_December_(Flight_day_11_\xe2\x80\x93_Undocking)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="19_December_.28Flight_day_11_.E2.80.93_Undocking.29">\n        19 December (Flight day 11 \xe2\x80\x93 Undocking)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-116&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: 19 December (Flight day 11 \xe2\x80\x93 Undocking)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-116_ANDE_Released_(S116-E-07828).jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2000" data-file-width="3032" height="145" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/STS-116_ANDE_Released_%28S116-E-07828%29.jpg/220px-STS-116_ANDE_Released_%28S116-E-07828%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/STS-116_ANDE_Released_%28S116-E-07828%29.jpg/330px-STS-116_ANDE_Released_%28S116-E-07828%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/STS-116_ANDE_Released_%28S116-E-07828%29.jpg/440px-STS-116_ANDE_Released_%28S116-E-07828%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-116_ANDE_Released_(S116-E-07828).jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         As seen through windows on the aft flight deck of Space Shuttle Discovery, a Department of Defense\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Picosatellite" title="Picosatellite">\n          picosatellite\n         </a>\n         known as Atmospheric Neutral Density Experiment (ANDE) is released from the shuttle\'s payload bay.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Flight day 11 began for the astronauts at approximately 14:47 UTC. The Expedition 14 and STS-116 crews posed for photos and then closed the hatches between the ISS and Discovery. Undocking was complete at 22:10 UTC. Due to the extended mission for EVA No. 4,\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       did not make a full circle to film and photograph ISS, but only flew slightly more than one-quarter of the way around (through ISS zenith) before its departure burn.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="20_December_(Flight_day_12)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="20_December_.28Flight_day_12.29">\n        20 December (Flight day 12)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-116&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: 20 December (Flight day 12)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Flight day 12 began for the astronauts at 12:48 UTC. They spent the day verifying the integrity of\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       \'s heat shield and preparing for deorbit and landing on 22 December 2006 (Flight day 14). Because of the extended spaceflight, the shuttle was required to make a landing attempt on flight day 14 unless all three landing sites were "no-go." Two satellites were also launched:\n       <b>\n        MEPSI\n       </b>\n       (Microelectromechanical System-Based PICOSAT Inspector) resembles a pair of tethered coffee-cups, and is being tested as a reconnaissance option for disabled satellites;\n       <b>\n        RAFT\n       </b>\n       (Radar Fence Transponder) is a pair of 5" cubes built by the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Naval_Academy" title="United States Naval Academy">\n        U.S. Naval Academy\n       </a>\n       which will test space radar systems and also act as data relays for mobile ground communications.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-STS116_mission_status_39-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-STS116_mission_status-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ANDE-RAFT_45-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ANDE-RAFT-45">\n         [45]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="21_December_(Flight_day_13)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="21_December_.28Flight_day_13.29">\n        21 December (Flight day 13)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-116&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: 21 December (Flight day 13)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Flight day 13 began for the astronauts at 12:17 UTC.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-116flightplan_35-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-116flightplan-35">\n         [35]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <i>\n        Discovery\'\n       </i>\n       s crew launched the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ANDE" title="ANDE">\n        ANDE\n       </a>\n       (Atmospheric Neutral Density Experiment) microsats for the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Naval_Research_Laboratory" title="Naval Research Laboratory">\n        Naval Research Laboratory\n       </a>\n       , which were designed to measure the density and composition of the low Earth orbit atmosphere in order to help better predict the movements of objects in orbit, but one of the satellites failed to emerge from its launch canister. ANDE is currently transmitting data, and emerged from the canister approximately 30 minutes after its launch according to satellite tracking data.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="22_December_(Flight_day_14_\xe2\x80\x93_Landing)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="22_December_.28Flight_day_14_.E2.80.93_Landing.29">\n        22 December (Flight day 14 \xe2\x80\x93 Landing)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-116&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: 22 December (Flight day 14 \xe2\x80\x93 Landing)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-116_landing.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2008" data-file-width="3000" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/STS-116_landing.jpg/220px-STS-116_landing.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/STS-116_landing.jpg/330px-STS-116_landing.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/STS-116_landing.jpg/440px-STS-116_landing.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-116_landing.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         STS-116 landing at KSC.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-116_landing_port_behind.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1173" data-file-width="1759" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/STS-116_landing_port_behind.jpg/220px-STS-116_landing_port_behind.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/STS-116_landing_port_behind.jpg/330px-STS-116_landing_port_behind.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d5/STS-116_landing_port_behind.jpg/440px-STS-116_landing_port_behind.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-116_landing_port_behind.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <i>\n          Discovery\n         </i>\n         following the landing chute deployment.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Flight day 14 began for the astronauts at 12:17 UTC. Preparations for landing were complete. High cross-winds precluded a landing at\n       <a href="/wiki/Edwards_Air_Force_Base" title="Edwards Air Force Base">\n        Edwards Air Force Base\n       </a>\n       while clouds and showers were an issue at\n       <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center" title="Kennedy Space Center">\n        Kennedy Space Center\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Shuttle_Landing_Facility" title="Shuttle Landing Facility">\n        Shuttle Landing Facility\n       </a>\n       on the first orbit. That combination raised the possibility of the first landing at\n       <a href="/wiki/White_Sands_Missile_Range" title="White Sands Missile Range">\n        White Sands Space Harbor\n       </a>\n       since\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-3" title="STS-3">\n        STS-3\n       </a>\n       in 1982.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-STS116_mission_status_39-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-STS116_mission_status-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Had landing taken place at White Sands, it could have taken as long as 60 days to return the orbiter to Kennedy Space Center. The first landing opportunity at Kennedy Space Center was abandoned due to unfavorable weather conditions. However, at 21:00 UTC coordinates were sent to the shuttle to re-attempt a landing at Kennedy along runway 15, as the first contingency landing attempt at Edwards had been scrubbed due to high cross winds. The de-orbit burn for Kennedy occurred at 21:27 UTC, having been authorized at 21:23 UTC, and was finished at 21:31 UTC. Since the landing time coincided with the local sunset time 17:32 EST (22:32 UTC), the shuttle landing was not considered a night landing, as official rules for a night landing are sunset + 15 minutes; however the\n       <a href="/wiki/Xenon_arc_lamp" title="Xenon arc lamp">\n        xenon\n       </a>\n       runway lighting system was in use.\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       touched down 30 seconds before the expected time. Landing time at Kennedy was at 17:32 EST (22:32 UTC).\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Contingency_planning">\n        Contingency planning\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-116&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Contingency planning">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-3xx" title="STS-3xx">\n        STS-3xx\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="STS-301">\n        STS-301\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-116&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: STS-301">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-3xx" title="STS-3xx">\n        STS-301\n       </a>\n       was the designation given to the\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-3xx" title="STS-3xx">\n        Contingency Shuttle Crew Support\n       </a>\n       mission which would have been launched in the event\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Atlantis" title="Space Shuttle Atlantis">\n        Space Shuttle\n        <i>\n         Atlantis\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       had become disabled during\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-115" title="STS-115">\n        STS-115\n       </a>\n       . It was a modified version of the STS-116 mission, which would have involved the launch date being brought forward. If needed, it would have launched no earlier than 11 November 2006. The crew for this mission was a four-person subset of the full STS-116 crew:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Mark_L._Polansky" title="Mark L. Polansky">\n         Mark Polansky\n        </a>\n        \xe2\x80\x93 Commander and prime\n        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Remote_Manipulator_System" title="Remote Manipulator System">\n         Remote Manipulator System\n        </a>\n        (RMS) operator\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/William_Oefelein" title="William Oefelein">\n         William Oefelein\n        </a>\n        \xe2\x80\x93 Pilot and backup RMS operator\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Robert_Curbeam" title="Robert Curbeam">\n         Robert Curbeam\n        </a>\n        \xe2\x80\x93 Mission specialist 1, Extravehicular 1\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Nicholas_Patrick" title="Nicholas Patrick">\n         Nicholas Patrick\n        </a>\n        \xe2\x80\x93 Mission specialist 2, Extravehicular 2\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="STS-317">\n        STS-317\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-116&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: STS-317">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       In the event that\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Discovery" title="Space Shuttle Discovery">\n         Discovery\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       suffered irreparable damage but made it to Earth orbit during STS-116, the crew would have taken refuge at the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">\n        ISS\n       </a>\n       and waited for a\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-3xx" title="STS-3xx">\n        Contingency Shuttle Crew Support\n       </a>\n       mission to launch. The mission would have been named\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-3xx" title="STS-3xx">\n        STS-317\n       </a>\n       and would have been flown by the\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Atlantis" title="Space Shuttle Atlantis">\n        Space Shuttle\n        <i>\n         Atlantis\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       no earlier than 21 February 2007. The crew for this rescue mission would have been a subset of the full\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-117" title="STS-117">\n        STS-117\n       </a>\n       crew.\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Wake-up_calls">\n        Wake-up calls\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-116&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Wake-up calls">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       A tradition for NASA spaceflights since the days of\n       <a href="/wiki/Project_Gemini" title="Project Gemini">\n        Gemini\n       </a>\n       , mission crews are played a special musical track at the start of each day in space. Each track is specially chosen, often by their family, and usually has special meaning to an individual member of the crew, or is applicable to their daily activities.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-46">\n        <a href="#cite_note-46">\n         [46]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        Day 2: "\n        <a href="/wiki/Here_Comes_the_Sun" title="Here Comes the Sun">\n         Here Comes the Sun\n        </a>\n        " by\n        <a href="/wiki/The_Beatles" title="The Beatles">\n         The Beatles\n        </a>\n        ; played for Commander Mark Polansky.\n        <a class="external text" href="http://spaceflight.nasa.gov/gallery/audio/shuttle/sts-116/mp3/fd02.mp3" rel="nofollow">\n         MP3\n        </a>\n        <a class="external text" href="http://spaceflight.nasa.gov/gallery/audio/shuttle/sts-116/wave/fd02.wav" rel="nofollow">\n         WAV\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Day 3: "Beep Beep" by\n        <a href="/wiki/Louis_Prima" title="Louis Prima">\n         Louis Prima\n        </a>\n        ; played for Sunita Williams.\n        <a class="external text" href="http://spaceflight.nasa.gov/gallery/audio/shuttle/sts-116/mp3/fd03.mp3" rel="nofollow">\n         MP3\n        </a>\n        <a class="external text" href="http://spaceflight.nasa.gov/gallery/audio/shuttle/sts-116/wave/fd03.wav" rel="nofollow">\n         WAV\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Day 4: "\n        <a href="/wiki/Waterloo_(ABBA_song)" title="Waterloo (ABBA song)">\n         Waterloo\n        </a>\n        " by\n        <a href="/wiki/ABBA" title="ABBA">\n         ABBA\n        </a>\n        ; played for Christer Fuglesang.\n        <a class="external text" href="http://spaceflight.nasa.gov/gallery/audio/shuttle/sts-116/mp3/fd04.mp3" rel="nofollow">\n         MP3\n        </a>\n        <a class="external text" href="http://spaceflight.nasa.gov/gallery/audio/shuttle/sts-116/wave/fd04.wav" rel="nofollow">\n         WAV\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Day 5: "\n        <a href="/wiki/Suavemente_(song)" title="Suavemente (song)">\n         Suavemente\n        </a>\n        " by\n        <a href="/wiki/Elvis_Crespo" title="Elvis Crespo">\n         Elvis Crespo\n        </a>\n        ; played for Joan Higginbotham.\n        <a class="external text" href="http://spaceflight.nasa.gov/gallery/audio/shuttle/sts-116/mp3/fd05.mp3" rel="nofollow">\n         MP3\n        </a>\n        <a class="external text" href="http://spaceflight.nasa.gov/gallery/audio/shuttle/sts-116/wave/fd05.wav" rel="nofollow">\n         WAV\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Day 6: "\n        <a href="/wiki/Under_Pressure" title="Under Pressure">\n         Under Pressure\n        </a>\n        " by\n        <a href="/wiki/Queen_(band)" title="Queen (band)">\n         Queen\n        </a>\n        &amp;\n        <a href="/wiki/David_Bowie" title="David Bowie">\n         David Bowie\n        </a>\n        ; Chosen as part of the EVA involved shaking the solar array. The track was used as a wake up call on\n        <a href="/wiki/STS-85" title="STS-85">\n         STS-85\n        </a>\n        when a Microgravity Vibration Isolation Mount was being tested. Curbeam was a mission specialist on that flight. It was his first trip into space.\n        <a class="external text" href="http://spaceflight.nasa.gov/gallery/audio/shuttle/sts-116/mp3/fd10.mp3" rel="nofollow">\n         MP3\n        </a>\n
